</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>Solve by “separating variables” method: arrange the equation so that all terms involving <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.464ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.109ex" height="1.464ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 490 647"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="79" d="M21 287Q21 301 36 335T84 406T158 442Q199 442 224 419T250 355Q248 336 247 334Q247 331 231 288T198 191T182 105Q182 62 196 45T238 27Q261 27 281 38T312 61T339 94Q339 95 344 114T358 173T377 247Q415 397 419 404Q432 431 462 431Q475 431 483 424T494 412T496 403Q496 390 447 193T391 -23Q363 -106 294 -155T156 -205Q111 -205 77 -183T43 -117Q43 -95 50 -80T69 -58T89 -48T106 -45Q150 -45 150 -87Q150 -107 138 -122T115 -142T102 -147L99 -148Q101 -153 118 -160T152 -167H160Q177 -167 186 -165Q219 -156 247 -127T290 -65T313 -9T321 21L315 17Q309 13 296 6T270 -6Q250 -11 231 -11Q185 -11 150 11T104 82Q103 89 103 113Q103 170 138 262T173 379Q173 380 173 381Q173 390 173 393T169 400T158 404H154Q131 404 112 385T82 344T65 302T57 280Q55 278 41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> are on one side and all terms involving <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.294ex" height="1.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 572 453"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="78" d="M52 289Q59 331 106 386T222 442Q257 442 286 424T329 379Q371 442 430 442Q467 442 494 420T522 361Q522 332 508 314T481 292T458 288Q439 288 427 299T415 328Q415 374 465 391Q454 404 425 404Q412 404 406 402Q368 386 350 336Q290 115 290 78Q290 50 306 38T341 26Q378 26 414 59T463 140Q466 150 469 151T485 153H489Q504 153 504 145Q504 144 502 134Q486 77 440 33T333 -11Q263 -11 227 52Q186 -10 133 -10H127Q78 -10 57 16T35 71Q35 103 54 123T99 143Q142 143 142 101Q142 81 130 66T107 46T94 41L91 40Q91 39 97 36T113 29T132 26Q168 26 194 71Q203 87 217 139T245 247T261 313Q266 340 266 352Q266 380 251 392T217 404Q177 404 142 372T93 290Q91 281 88 280T72 278H58Q52 284 52 289Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> are on the other side, then integrate both sides.</div>
<hr style="border:1px solid red" >
</details>

<div>Integrate both sides:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -2.016ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48.539ex" height="5.432ex" role="img" focusable="false" <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.464ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="5.257ex" height="1.971ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2323.6 871"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="79" d="M21 287Q21 301 36 335T84 406T158 442Q199 442 224 419T250 355Q248 336 247 334Q247 331 231 288T198 191T182 105Q182 62 196 45T238 27Q261 27 281 38T312 61T339 94Q339 95 344 114T358 173T377 247Q415 397 419 404Q432 431 462 431Q475 431 483 424T494 412T496 403Q496 390 447 193T391 -23Q363 -106 294 -155T156 -205Q111 -205 77 -183T43 -117Q43 -95 50 -80T69 -58T89 -48T106 -45Q150 -45 150 -87Q150 -107 138 -122T115 -142T102 -147L99 -148Q101 -153 118 -160T152 -167H160Q177 -167 186 -165Q219 -156 247 -127T290 -65T313 -9T321 21L315 17Q309 13 296 6T270 -6Q250 -11 231 -11Q185 -11 150 11T104 82Q103 89 103 113Q103 170 138 262T173 379Q173 380 173 381Q173 390 173 393T169 400T158 404H154Q131 404 112 385T82 344T65 302T57 280Q55 278 41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(767.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1823.6, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> when <span class="math-inline ">

(There is no need to express <span class="math-inline ">

<div>Thus a particular (implicit) solution is</div>

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>Try to find a way to separate the variables <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.294ex" height="1.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 572 453"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="78" d="M52 289Q59 331 106 386T222 442Q257 442 286 424T329 379Q371 442 430 442Q467 442 494 420T522 361Q522 332 508 314T481 292T458 288Q439 288 427 299T415 328Q415 374 465 391Q454 404 425 404Q412 404 406 402Q368 386 350 336Q290 115 290 78Q290 50 306 38T341 26Q378 26 414 59T463 140Q466 150 469 151T485 153H489Q504 153 504 145Q504 144 502 134Q486 77 440 33T333 -11Q263 -11 227 52Q186 -10 133 -10H127Q78 -10 57 16T35 71Q35 103 54 123T99 143Q142 143 142 101Q142 81 130 66T107 46T94 41L91 40Q91 39 97 36T113 29T132 26Q168 26 194 71Q203 87 217 139T245 247T261 313Q266 340 266 352Q266 380 251 392T217 404Q177 404 142 372T93 290Q91 281 88 280T72 278H58Q52 284 52 289Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.464ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.109ex" height="1.464ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 490 647"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="79" d="M21 287Q21 301 36 335T84 406T158 442Q199 442 224 419T250 355Q248 336 247 334Q247 331 231 288T198 191T182 105Q182 62 196 45T238 27Q261 27 281 38T312 61T339 94Q339 95 344 114T358 173T377 247Q415 397 419 404Q432 431 462 431Q475 431 483 424T494 412T496 403Q496 390 447 193T391 -23Q363 -106 294 -155T156 -205Q111 -205 77 -183T43 -117Q43 -95 50 -80T69 -58T89 -48T106 -45Q150 -45 150 -87Q150 -107 138 -122T115 -142T102 -147L99 -148Q101 -153 118 -160T152 -167H160Q177 -167 186 -165Q219 -156 247 -127T290 -65T313 -9T321 21L315 17Q309 13 296 6T270 -6Q250 -11 231 -11Q185 -11 150 11T104 82Q103 89 103 113Q103 170 138 262T173 379Q173 380 173 381Q173 390 173 393T169 400T158 404H154Q131 404 112 385T82 344T65 302T57 280Q55 278 41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>. <li>At time <span class="math-inline ">

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>Since the rate of increase is proportional to the concentration:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -1.577ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="15.042ex" height="4.701ex" role="img" focusable="false" <div>where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.179ex" height="1.595ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -694 521 705"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="6B" d="M121 647Q121 657 125 670T137 683Q138 683 209 688T282 694Q294 694 294 686Q294 679 244 477Q194 279 194 272Q213 282 223 291Q247 309 292 354T362 415Q402 442 438 442Q468 442 485 423T503 369Q503 344 496 327T477 302T456 291T438 288Q418 288 406 299T394 328Q394 353 410 369T442 390L458 393Q446 405 434 405H430Q398 402 367 380T294 316T228 255Q230 254 243 252T267 246T293 238T320 224T342 206T359 180T365 147Q365 130 360 106T354 66Q354 26 381 26Q429 26 459 145Q461 153 479 153H483Q499 153 499 144Q499 139 496 130Q455 -11 378 -11Q333 -11 305 15T277 90Q277 108 280 121T283 145Q283 167 269 183T234 206T200 217T182 220H180Q168 178 159 139T145 81T136 44T129 20T122 7T111 -2Q98 -11 83 -11Q66 -11 57 -1T48 16Q48 26 85 176T158 471L195 616Q196 629 188 632T149 637H144Q134 637 131 637T124 640T121 647Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is a constant. Solve by separating variables method. Then use the initial conditions to find the constants.</div>
<hr style="border:1px solid red" >
</details>
<br>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solution</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>Since the rate of increase is proportional to the concentration:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.179ex" height="1.595ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -694 521 705"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="6B" d="M121 647Q121 657 125 670T137 683Q138 683 209 688T282 694Q294 694 294 686Q294 679 244 477Q194 279 194 272Q213 282 223 291Q247 309 292 354T362 415Q402 442 438 442Q468 442 485 423T503 369Q503 344 496 327T477 302T456 291T438 288Q418 288 406 299T394 328Q394 353 410 369T442 390L458 393Q446 405 434 405H430Q398 402 367 380T294 316T228 255Q230 254 243 252T267 246T293 238T320 224T342 206T359 180T365 147Q365 130 360 106T354 66Q354 26 381 26Q429 26 459 145Q461 153 479 153H483Q499 153 499 144Q499 139 496 130Q455 -11 378 -11Q333 -11 305 15T277 90Q277 108 280 121T283 145Q283 167 269 183T234 206T200 217T182 220H180Q168 178 159 139T145 81T136 44T129 20T122 7T111 -2Q98 -11 83 -11Q66 -11 57 -1T48 16Q48 26 85 176T158 471L195 616Q196 629 188 632T149 637H144Q134 637 131 637T124 640T121 647Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is a constant.</div>
<div>Separate variables and integrate:</div>

<div>Integral both sides:</div>

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >

<div>Taking logarithms (or using base‑5 logs),</div>

<div>(b) How long does it take for the container to empty completely?</div>

<br>
<ol start="7">
<li>The rate at which a body loses temperature at any instant is proportional to the amount by which the temperature of the body, at that instant, exceeds the temperature of its surroundings.<br>
A cup of tea is in a room. The ambient temperature of the room is <span class="math-inline ">

<div>Separate variables and integrate:</div>

<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="37.691ex" height="2.23ex" role="img" focusable="false" <div>(b) Suggest one limitation of this model.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>It requires that the ambient temperature remains constant. In reality, the ambient temperature may vary over time.</div>
<hr style="border:1px solid red" >
</details>
